PART   I :  SEC .  (I) – GAZETTE OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA – 29.06.2007
IMPORTANT NOTICE REGARDING ACCEPTANCE OF NOTICES
 FOR PUBLICATION IN THE WEEKLY "GAZETTE"
ATTENTION is drawn to each  of the Notices appearing in the 1st week of every month, regarding the latest dates and time of acceptance
of notices for publication in the weekly Gazette  at the end of each Part of the Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.
All notices to be published in every Part of the Gazette shall close at 12 noon of each Friday, a fortnight before the date of
publication. All Departments, Corporations, Boards, etc.,  are advised that any notification fixing specific dates for closing times of
applications  in regard to vacancies, tender notices and the dates and times of auction sales, etc.,   should be prepared with due regard
to this change, i.e. by  giving adequate time both from the time of despatch of notice  to the Government Press and from the date of
publication thus enabling those interested in the contents of the notices to actively and positively participate.
All notices to be published in the weekly Gazette  should reach this Department positively by 12 noon of the Friday, two
weeks prior to date of publication e.g., Notices for publication in the weekly Gazette of  06th  July, 2007  should reach the Government
Press on or before 12  noon on 22nd June, 2007.
L AKSHMAN   GOONEWARDENA ,
Government Printer.
Department of Govt. Printing,
Colombo 08,
January 01, 2007.
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka

(Published by Authority)

PART   I :  SEC .  (I) – GAZETTE OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA – 29.06.2007
Miscellaneous Departmental Notices
HATTON   NATIONAL   BANK   LIMITED–
AMBALANGODA
Resolution adopted by the Board of Directors of Hatton
National Bank Limited under Section 4 of the Recovery of
Loans by Banks  (Special Provisions) Act No. 04 of 1990
AT a meeting of the Board of Directors of  Hatton National Bank
Limited held on 24th May 2007 it was resolved specially and
unanimously :
“Whereas Rohan De Vas Gunasekara as the Obligor has made
default in payment due on Bond No. 4860 and 5187 dated 20th
November 1998 and 07th May 2002 respectively both
attested by A. M. Bandularathna Notary Public of Ambalangoda
in favour of Hatton National Bank Limited and there is now due
and owing to the Hatton National Bank Limited as at 28th February
2007 a sum of Rupees One Million Nine Hundred and Twenty Six
Thousand One Hundred and Seventy Five and Cents Eighty Three
(Rs. 1,926,175.83) on the said Bonds and the Board of Directors
of Hatton National Bank Limited under the power vested by the
Recovery of Loans by Banks (Special Provisions) Act No.04 of
1990, do hereby resolve that the property and premises morefully
described in the schedule, hereto and mortgaged to Hatton National
Bank Limited by the said Bond Nos. 4860 and 5187 be sold by
Public Auction by N. H. P. F. Ariyaratne Licensed Auctioneer of
Colombo for recovery of the said sum of Rs. 544,619 together with
further interest from 1st March 2007 to date of sale together with
costs of advertising and other charges incurred less payments (if
any) since received.
THE  SCHEDULE  ABOVE  REFERRED TO
1. All that difined and divided allotment of land called “Lot 2A of
Lot 2 of Lots B, C and D of Mahagedarawatta” together with all
plantations buildings and everything standing  thereon and bearing
Assessment No. 323/9, New Road, Ward No.2, Urban Council
Amabalangoda and situated at Patabendimulla in Ambalangoda in the
Wellaboda Pattu of Galle District, southern Province and bounded on
the North by Lot 1 of Lots B, C and D of Mahagedarawatta and
Pelawatte: East by Endowadarala Padinchiwaunwatta (more correctrly
lots 3 and 4 of Gedarawatta); South by lot 4 of Lots B, C and D of
Mahagedarawatta and Lot 2B of the same land and West by Lot 2B
of the same land and Lot 1 of  Lots B, C and D of Mahagedarawatta
and containing  in extent Seven decimal Five Perches (0A., 0R., 7.5P)
as depicted in Plan No. 265 dated 5th January 1974 made by Mr. A.
G. F. Perera of Ambalangoda, Licensed Surveyor, Registered under
Title A 79/202, Land Registry, Balapitiya.
2. All that defined and divided allotment of land called Lot 3 of
Gedarawatta  as per recent Plan of Survey No. 538 dated 11th January
1997 made by Mr. P. H. D. Silva of Ambalangoda, Licensed Surveyor

 HATTON   NATIONAL   BANK   LIMITED
GRANDPASS  BRANCH
Resolution adopted by  the  Board  of Directors of Hatton
National Bank  Limited under Section  4 of the  Recovery of
Loans by Banks (Special Provisions) Act, No. 04 of 1990
AT a meeting of the Board  of Directors of Hatton National Bank
Limited held  on 24th May  2007  it was resolved specially and
unanimously:
“Whereas  Kandasamy selvarajah Sole Proprietor of “ S. K.
Merchants “ as the Obligor  has  made  default in payment due on
Bond No. 1466 dated 5th January 2006 attested by B. D. T.
Dharmatilleke Notary Public of Colombo  in favour  of Hatton
National Bank  Limited  and  there  is now  due and owing  to the
Hatton National Bank  Limited  as at 28 th  February 2007  a sum
of Rupees Three Million One  Thousand One Hundred and Fifteen
Cents Ninety One  (Rs.  3,001,115.91) on the said  Bonds and the
Board of Directors of Hatton  National Bank  Limited under the
power vested by the Revovery of Loans by Banks  (Special
Provisions) Act, No. 4 of 1990, do hereby resolve that the
property and premises morefully described in teh  Schedule,
hereto and mertgaged to Hatton National Bank  Limited  by the
said   Bond  No. 1466 be  sold  by Public Auction by R. S.
Mahanama Licensed Auctioneer of Colombo  for recovery of  the
said  sum of Rs. 3.001,115. 91 together  with further interest
from  1st March 2007 to date  of sale  together with costs of
advertising and other charges incurred less payments (if any)
since received.
